\hypertarget{classTMPro_1_1TMP__Text}{}\doxysection{T\+M\+Pro.\+T\+M\+P\+\_\+\+Text Class Reference}
\label{classTMPro_1_1TMP__Text}\index{TMPro.TMP\_Text@{TMPro.TMP\_Text}}

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Base class which contains common properties and functions shared between the \mbox{\hyperlink{classTMPro_1_1TextMeshPro}{Text\+Mesh\+Pro}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classTMPro_1_1TextMeshProUGUI}{Text\+Mesh\+Pro\+U\+G\+UI}} component.
